I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

**GT expression:**
`0.8677806610632854*(-1 + P/6.057935627201261)*(1 - P/14.185052779605893)*P + 0.8677806610632854*P^(1/3) + 0.8677806610632854*P`

Let me expand the first term:
`(-1 + P/6.058)(1 - P/14.185)*P`

Let me expand `(-1 + P/6.058)(1 - P/14.185)`:
= `-1 + P/14.185 + P/6.058 - P²/(6.058*14.185)`
= `-1 + P(1/14.185 + 1/6.058) - P²/85.91`

Multiply by P:
= `-P + P²(1/14.185 + 1/6.058) - P³/85.91`

So the full GT becomes:
`0.8678*[-P + P²(1/14.185 + 1/6.058) - P³/85.91] + 0.8678*P^(1/3) + 0.8678*P`

The `-P` and `+P` terms (both multiplied by 0.8678) cancel!

GT = `0.8678*P^(1/3) + 0.8678*P²*(1/14.185 + 1/6.058) - 0.8678*P³/85.91`

Computing: 1/14.185 + 1/6.058 ≈ 0.0705 + 0.1651 = 0.2356

So GT = `c₀*P^(1/3) + c₁*P² + c₂*P³`

where c₀ = 0.8678, c₁ = 0.8678*0.2356 ≈ 0.2045, c₂ = -0.8678/85.91 ≈ -0.01010

**GT simplifies to: a*P^(1/3) + b*P² + c*P³**
